  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0d92f159-3233-4b3b-a3e8-1b475899f19f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer6610654317317286776">In the beginning, there was him. <br/><br/>Gutsy, green-eyed Eleanor never met a rule she didn't want to break. She's sick of her mother's zealotry and the confines of Catholic school, and declares she'll never go to church again. But her first glimpse of beautiful, magnetic Father Marcus Stearns and his lust-worthy Italian motorcycle is an epiphany. Suddenly, daily Mass seems like </span>
  <span id="freeText6610654317317286776" style="display:none">In the beginning, there was him. <br /><br />Gutsy, green-eyed Eleanor never met a rule she didn't want to break. She's sick of her mother's zealotry and the confines of Catholic school, and declares she'll never go to church again. But her first glimpse of beautiful, magnetic Father Marcus Stearns and his lust-worthy Italian motorcycle is an epiphany. Suddenly, daily Mass seems like a reward, and her punishment is the ache she feels when they're apart. He is intelligent and insightful and he seems to know her intimately at her very core. Eleanor is consumed—and even she knows that can't be right. <br /><br />But when one desperate mistake nearly costs Eleanor everything, it is Søren who steps in to save her. She vows to repay him with complete obedience…and a whole world opens before her as he reveals to her his deepest secrets. <br /><br />Danger can be managed—pain, welcomed. Everything is about to begin.</span>

<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/44009567-ja-onna-wilson"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1434462881i/44009567._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/44009567-ja-onna-wilson">Ja&#39;Onna Wilson</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The book gets better. The white series is about Nora recounting her days as a submissive to soren, the memories are very rich, colorful and humorous. <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The book gets better. The white series is about Nora recounting her days as a submissive to soren, the memories are very rich, colorful and humorous. Yeah, when the book goes back to the present it does become a little depressing but the memories are really good. I must say, this book took me off guard, I finished the last book thinking everyone won and was happy. This beginning was a rude awakening, I'm still not sure how it all happened with Soren dying and all. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer516242991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16943835545581146532"><b>5+ Stars!!!</b> <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/f4f6a7fd-96be-449b-adf4-72f478e97334_zpse7077e1f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697861.jpg' alt=' photo f4f6a7fd-96be-449b-adf4-72f478e97334_zpse7077e1f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Just when I find myself thinking Tiffany’s books can’t get any better I am proven wrong. If only we would have had this book first, I think everyone would have had such a different opinion of Søren. I loved the way this story was told. In mostly flashbacks from Nora. I hope all the installments of the White Years are told exactly this way. As a bedtime story so to speak. <br/><br/>Anyone who’s read The Original Sinners series knows that Eleanor was a troubled youth. Things with both parent</span>
  <span id="freeText16943835545581146532" style="display:none"><b>5+ Stars!!!</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/f4f6a7fd-96be-449b-adf4-72f478e97334_zpse7077e1f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697861.jpg" alt=" photo f4f6a7fd-96be-449b-adf4-72f478e97334_zpse7077e1f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Just when I find myself thinking Tiffany’s books can’t get any better I am proven wrong. If only we would have had this book first, I think everyone would have had such a different opinion of Søren. I loved the way this story was told. In mostly flashbacks from Nora. I hope all the installments of the White Years are told exactly this way. As a bedtime story so to speak. <br><br>Anyone who’s read The Original Sinners series knows that Eleanor was a troubled youth. Things with both parents weren’t great and she found herself in a little bit of trouble more than once. She never thought she would find someone to save her. Someone who cared for her so much that they would do anything to protect her, to keep her safe. She really didn’t think she would find this man at church. <br><i>
  <blockquote>This man, this most beautiful man she’d ever seen in her life, this man who was the incarnation of her every hunger, every desire and every secret midnight dream... This man was her new priest?</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/bb543cc5-46bc-4dc5-87f1-75897f7baa75_zpsd5dca9b5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697862.jpg" alt=" photo bb543cc5-46bc-4dc5-87f1-75897f7baa75_zpsd5dca9b5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>From Nora’s teenage years all the way until she is twenty we get to see her relationship with Søren. We see how much he really did help her and mold her into the woman she is now. Nora is and has always been fabulous, but the path she was headed towards wasn’t the best. Søren was there as an ear to listen, a person to talk to, and he made her aspire to do better. To be a better person. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Whatever this game is we’re playing, I’m going to win it.” <br><br>“If you trust me and obey me, we might both win.”</blockquote>
</i> Nora quickly realizes that Søren isn’t playing games with her. She falls deeper and deeper in love with him as time passes. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b6a64c24-1ab7-4a85-aa1c-9755ee4803f5_zpsf1cc11a2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697863.jpg" alt=" photo b6a64c24-1ab7-4a85-aa1c-9755ee4803f5_zpsf1cc11a2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I may not have been the biggest Søren fan from the beginning. When I first read <i>The Siren</i>, I had mixed feelings about him. As the series went on, I grew to love him. In this book, I had nothing but love for Søren. I think even those who don’t care for him will fall hard for him here. There love really is inspiring. <br><br>I will still gladly proclaim Nora as my favorite heroine ever. She is so spunky and fun. I will never grow tired of reading of her. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b684b31e-5b19-4090-a72a-37c93e507bdd_zps1d344968.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697864.jpg" alt=" photo b684b31e-5b19-4090-a72a-37c93e507bdd_zps1d344968.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is also an element of mystery to <i>The Saint</i>. Though the story focus’s on the past, primarily Nora and Søren’s relationship, I found myself wondering why Nora was where she was and why she was with the person she was with. There are a few things left open, but no cliffhanger. <br><br>I don’t care what crazy things happen or what gets thrown in their way, I still firmly believe that Nora and Søren are a couple that is truly meant to be. They’ve been through their fair share of obstacles. Their relationship is far from perfect and their love story is far from conventional, but it is still so beautiful.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/ff1e7c9f-0f09-41b1-b148-b924b92c8463_zpse5a22a91.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697865.jpg" alt=" photo ff1e7c9f-0f09-41b1-b148-b924b92c8463_zpse5a22a91.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This series is original, addictive and brilliant. The writing is stunning. Tiffany Reisz is an autobuy author for me. If she writes it, I will read it. And the fact that the next book is about one of my favorite characters, Kingsley Edge, makes me even more excited to continue on this journey. I loved all the Kingsly we got in this story and I can’t wait for more! <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You mind-fucked me.”<br><br>“Does your brain hurt? I tired to be gentle since it was your first time.”</blockquote>
</i><br> This is a book and series you won’t want to miss out on! If you haven’t read them yet, I can’t recommend them enough. And if you’ve already read The Original Sinners series, you won’t be disappointed with this!<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Every choice has a price. Sometimes we don’t know what it is until after we’ve paid it.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/c5e6a4d5-03b3-4875-9fcd-c1f0f0240556_zps2bb6f7a8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400617494i/9697866.jpg" alt=" photo c5e6a4d5-03b3-4875-9fcd-c1f0f0240556_zps2bb6f7a8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Your nightmare might turn into your best dream someday.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <i>**ARC kindly provided by Harlequin via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.**</i></span>

<div id="review_935199642" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/935199642" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/935199642?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780263245981" href="/book/show/21082347-the-saint">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=advance-copy">advance-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=hot">hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=my-top-reads">my-top-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer935199642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11523720282446553243"><b>It's LIVE everywhere!<br/> Grab an AMAZING read or start the series! <br/>#EpicForbiddenLove</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400106310i/9635812.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And begin it did!! WOW!! This book is just, WOW. SO, so good. Tiffany Reisz NEVER fails. I didn't want the experience to end; it gave me a book hangover to end all book hangovers!<br/><br/><b>This is a, no ordinary love story from Tiffany Reisz.... </b><br/><br/>Tiffany Reisz has her very own brand of magic in The Original Sinners series. It's exciting, deliciously erotic, gripping, intense and so very, very moving. The effortless writing is</span>
  <span id="freeText11523720282446553243" style="display:none"><b>It's LIVE everywhere!<br> Grab an AMAZING read or start the series! <br>#EpicForbiddenLove</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400106310i/9635812.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And begin it did!! WOW!! This book is just, WOW. SO, so good. Tiffany Reisz NEVER fails. I didn't want the experience to end; it gave me a book hangover to end all book hangovers!<br><br><b>This is a, no ordinary love story from Tiffany Reisz.... </b><br><br>Tiffany Reisz has her very own brand of magic in The Original Sinners series. It's exciting, deliciously erotic, gripping, intense and so very, very moving. The effortless writing is simply stunning and offers the most all consuming, wonderful reading experience. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400874628i/9731454._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Saint</b> takes us to the beginning of the sinners story, to a time when fate brings 3 amazing, unique people together, Soren, Nora and Kingsley. Tiffany Reisz takes us on another epic, intense journey where we see their beautiful, dark story unfold. It’s not just a telling of the early years, the present day, 36 year old Nora, is weaved in with a suspenseful element, as she retells her very own fairy tale.... <i>it’s awe inspiring! </i> The transitions between past and present are seamless. <br><br><b>I have so much LOVE and affection for this series, this book and, of course, the main characters…. Soren, Nora and Kingsley. </b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“There is God, there is you and there is Kingsley. Those are my three nonnegotiables.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I’m not going tell you much more about the story, instead I'll try and translate my feelings, feelings that you'll be familiar with if you've read and loved the series, and if you haven't, I hope it makes you want to pick it up and devour! <br><br>As with all Original Sinners books, <b>The Saint</b> needs to be experienced firsthand, as it unfolds. Furthermore, there’s so much complexity to it, steeped in years of intertwining relationships that span decades. If you’ve read the previous books you’ll understand exactly what I mean! It probably took me a book and a novella before I began warming towards <i>Team Soren.</i> It wasn’t instant book love, more like vivid curiosity of their world and a love of spectacular erotic writing that got my attention…. But, a book love that grows, isn’t that the best kind? And.…Oh. My. Goodness, I’m in book love with Soren and all that he is. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400876683i/9731700._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a complex world, a world of submission and dominance taken to the extreme, with characters that give each other the freedom and space to be who they desire. SO many emotions, the author could take the story any which way, her characters could do many things, and I would go with it, accept it, and make moral exceptions,<i> that’s the power of her writing.</i> The characters have motivation and reason for everything, even if at first the behavioural reasons are not obvious.<b> This story and the characters have total acceptance from me. I relax, I read, immerse myself and totally adore!</b><br><br>Soren and Nora have the most moving heart to heart; it's wonderful, moving, reverent and heartbreaking. Their words are so passionate, so emotive, wrapped up in a story so intensely deep with layer upon layer; one sentence has the depth to move me to tears because the meaningfully soaked words have the power to effortlessly transport me to a feeling or thought from a previous book in the<i> Sinners</i> series. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400104832i/9635619._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>So very, very beautiful....</i><br><br><b>The Saint</b> made me totally understand how and why Nora and Soren came together and, if I had any doubts at all about the motivations of Soren, which I didn’t, just for the record, then The Saint seals it and gives complete understanding of his love, adoration and motivation. <br><br>Soren,<b> “…you’re the most beautiful man on earth.”</b> He's so wise, so all-knowing, everything he does, and everything he says is with love in his heart. <i>My heart </i>melted at the words and actions of Soren. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400874628i/9731455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We experience Nora growing into an intelligent, fearless, kind and caring woman. <b>“Your mind must be the most marvelous playground.” </b>We see the emergence of her sexual proclivities, her complete wants and desires. I love Nora’s sense of humour, her irony and her sarcastic wit. Such a fantastic heroine, still one of my all time favourite leading ladies!<br><br>The discussions about Catholicism at times made me smile, being a Catholic myself, I completely ‘got’ the meaning, and then at other times the discussion on the subject would touch my heart and make me feel just so desperately sad....<i> the enormity of a vocation?</i> But as the story so eloquently promotes, there's a reason for everything, a higher and a greater good…. It’s making me teary just thinking about their situation…… <i>So good. </i><br><br>Kingsley, his presence is charismatic and inspiring…. And so very important to this story.<br><br>*** <br><br>These books need to be experienced. Until you experience them you cannot truly comprehend the brilliance and complexity of emotions that this story evokes. The intertwining layers, the depth of the characters, and their relationship to each other, that spans over so many years. <br><br><b>Is this the greatest forbidden love story of all time?</b><i> I think… YES!</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400856951i/9728651._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In true Tiffany Reisz style there's something that's had me and my friends in high discussion! If you’ve read <b>The Saint</b> and want to take a peak at our spoilers or add your perspective, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/43464633#comment_form" rel="nofollow noopener">click here.</a> One thing is for sure we’re all highly anticipating the next installment in The Original Sinners series. <i>Still so much to discover. </i><br><br>If you're yet to experience the TOS world, and you love stories that push the boundaries of morality, make you think, are soaked in dark, BDSM themes, and highly erotic then you seriously need to jump on board with this series and immerse yourself in the unique world of<b> The Original Sinners</b>. <i> It's a very special series.</i><br><br><br><b>Note: The Saint is book one of the White years, but in my opinion it’s best experienced after The Mistress.</b><br><br><i>The following is the order in which I read and adored this series….</i>The 4 full length books are essential reading and the novellas, not to be missed.....<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532.The_Siren__The_Original_Sinners___1_" title="The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1335832751s/10970532.jpg" alt="The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9772406.The_Gift__The_Original_Sinners___0_5_" title="The Gift (The Original Sinners, #0.5) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1328364378s/9772406.jpg" alt="The Gift (The Original Sinners, #0.5) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18242114.Daniel_Part_Two__The_Original_Sinners___3_1_" title="Daniel Part Two (The Original Sinners, #3.1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/book/50x75-6121bf4c1f669098041843ec9650ca19.png" alt="Daniel Part Two (The Original Sinners, #3.1) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13548075.The_Angel__The_Original_Sinners___2_" title="The Angel (The Original Sinners, #2) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1337044736s/13548075.jpg" alt="The Angel (The Original Sinners, #2) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13540911.Little_Red_Riding_Crop__The_Original_Sinners___0_6_" title="Little Red Riding Crop (The Original Sinners, #0.6) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704494.Submit_to_Desire__The_Original_Sinners___0_7_" title="Submit to Desire (The Original Sinners, #0.7) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1339618603s/15704494.jpg" alt="Submit to Desire (The Original Sinners, #0.7) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704485.The_Prince__The_Original_Sinners___3_" title="The Prince (The Original Sinners, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1344776840s/15704485.jpg" alt="The Prince (The Original Sinners, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17251444.The_Mistress__The_Original_Sinners___4_" title="The Mistress (The Original Sinners, #4) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400273.Scars_and_Stripes__The_Last_Good_Knight___1_" title="Scars and Stripes (The Last Good Knight, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21468417.Sore_Spots__The_Last_Good_Knight___2_" title="Sore Spots (The Last Good Knight, #2) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395075943s/21468417.jpg" alt="Sore Spots (The Last Good Knight, #2) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21468414.The_Games_Destiny_Plays__The_Last_Good_Knight___3_" title="The Games Destiny Plays (The Last Good Knight, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395076003s/21468414.jpg" alt="The Games Destiny Plays (The Last Good Knight, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21468416.Fit_to_Be_Tied__The_Last_Good_Knight___4_" title="Fit to Be Tied (The Last Good Knight, #4) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395076055s/21468416.jpg" alt="Fit to Be Tied (The Last Good Knight, #4) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21468415.The_Last_Good_Night__The_Last_Good_Knight___5_" title="The Last Good Night (The Last Good Knight, #5) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395076097s/21468415.jpg" alt="The Last Good Night (The Last Good Knight, #5) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16117368.The_Saint__The_Original_Sinners_White_Years___1_" title="The Saint (The Original Sinners White Years, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1396028000s/16117368.jpg" alt="The Saint (The Original Sinners White Years, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>It worked beautifully for me!<br><br><br>♥ BR with Deanna, Irene &amp; TeriLyn <br><br>Complimentary copy provided by Harlequin, via NetGalley, for an honest review<br><br></span>

<div id="review_884218248" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/884218248" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884218248?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19311457-the-saint">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=6">6</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=doms-n-kink">doms-n-kink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=alpha">alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=unforgettables">unforgettables</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=love-story">love-story</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884218248" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer201561011856993892"><i>6 intoxicating stars</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355700._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Unfortunately, there’s no way to tell you the story of Kingsley and me without telling you the story of Søren and me,” she said. “It’s all one story, the three of us.”<br/><br/>“Will it hurt to talk about it?”<br/><br/>“Yes,” she said. “But a little pain never stopped me before.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>This was the beginning to an epic tale of love beyond measure. I can't tell you how much I LOVE this series, and to be able to live through how it all started just made it feel even more like a gift. Søren,</span>
  <span id="freeText201561011856993892" style="display:none"><i>6 intoxicating stars</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355700._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Unfortunately, there’s no way to tell you the story of Kingsley and me without telling you the story of Søren and me,” she said. “It’s all one story, the three of us.”<br><br>“Will it hurt to talk about it?”<br><br>“Yes,” she said. “But a little pain never stopped me before.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This was the beginning to an epic tale of love beyond measure. I can't tell you how much I LOVE this series, and to be able to live through how it all started just made it feel even more like a gift. Søren, Elle and Kinglsey are larger than life, there will never be anyone like them and there will never be a story such as theirs. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>‘rarely alone, never two, always three.’</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>BDSM is not what they do, but it's who they are, very much ingrained as part of their soul. <br><br><b>
  <u>Eleanor, Elle, Little One</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re gonna kill me with that, aren’t you?” <br><br>“Very likely.” <br><br>“I can think of worse ways to die.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355701._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Søren</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Eleanor, you joked about us breaking the table during sex. I don’t break furniture during sex. I break people.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355702.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Kingsley Edge</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You mind-fucked me.”<br><br>“Does your brain hurt? I tried to be gentle since it was your first time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355703._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nothing could have prepared me for their <i>first</i> kiss...nothing could have prepared me for their <i>first</i> time. It was beautiful, a true union of mated souls and I couldn't have imagined it any other way. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If it had been fire, I would have walked through fire,” she whispered.<br><br>“If it had been fire, I would have carried you through it.” He lifted her and laid her in the center of the bed.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457413766i/18355704._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Saint</b> was intoxicating, there really is not other word to describe it, I was a bit hesitant delving deeper into their minds, but in the end I found my worries were for naught. I feel like it just solidified everything I felt and more. Regardless that it was a story that was re-told, it still felt like I traveled back to that time, living each moment with them. There is so much to this story, love, light, pain, darkness, humor and banter making it truly unforgettable!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="201561011856993892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1165871557" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1165871557" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1165871557?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19311457-the-saint">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=tiffany-reisz-is-godsent">tiffany-reisz-is-godsent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=top-2015-reads">top-2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=panty-soaking-wet">panty-soaking-wet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=smartass-witty-banters">smartass-witty-banters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=books-i-d-have-babies-with">books-i-d-have-babies-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=forbidden-taboo-love">forbidden-taboo-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1165871557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7517114004210854462"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424591756i/13781017.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Once there lived…a priest.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>When I pick up a Tiffany Reisz book, I <i>know</i> I will never be left disappointed. And damn right because with <b>The Saint</b>, I couldn't even put it down for a minute as the queen of literary erotica that is TR has got me on a tight leash as I get reacquainted with The Original Sinners. There really is nothing that comes close to the Eighth Circle world that she has created and with her alluring writing that seemed so effortless, I simply cannot bring myself</span>
  <span id="freeText7517114004210854462" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424591756i/13781017.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Once there lived…a priest.”</i>
</b><br><br>When I pick up a Tiffany Reisz book, I <i>know</i> I will never be left disappointed. And damn right because with <b>The Saint</b>, I couldn't even put it down for a minute as the queen of literary erotica that is TR has got me on a tight leash as I get reacquainted with The Original Sinners. There really is nothing that comes close to the Eighth Circle world that she has created and with her alluring writing that seemed so effortless, I simply cannot bring myself to rate anything less than 5 stars when it comes to her work.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I wish I could give you everything you wanted. But even a good gift is a bad gift if given at the wrong time.”</i>
</blockquote> <br>Tuck up nicely kids because <u>The Saint</u> is going to be a bedtime story you'll wanna hear. We've always known that Nora led a troubled youth but we never got the full backstory of it. Told in alternating past/present mode, Nora reminisces and takes us back on the journey of how a young rebellious girl fell in love with that hot new priest in town. This is <i>
  <b>the story</b>
</i> we've been all waiting for.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424593904i/13781220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If I didn't adore adult Nora enough already, I absolutely LOVED young Nora. Spunky and feisty little spitfire she was, it's no wonder a man as commanding as Søren couldn't let this girl out of his sight. I was swooped away by their smart yet playful interactions that sometimes even brought out a side of Søren that leaves you a little surprised. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“What's a dissertation?"<br><br>"If Satan gave you instructions for writing the book report from Hell, it would closely resemble those of a Ph.D. dissertation.”</i>
</blockquote> <br>Being able to see how their relationship evolved over the time with the introduction of Kingsley, it truly solidify my love for all these characters. It was such a nice touch finally being able to understand all the little references from the earlier series such as the back of the Rolls Royce and how the name Sutherlin came around, that for me was such an added bonus to an already amazing read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424596429i/13781537.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is no ordinary love story that TR tells but it's just one that is so powerful and unique, one where doesn't leave me to question the moral aspects and to just embrace this one-of-a-kind love that leaves me with flutters and even moved me to tears! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[OMG Nora's birthday-orchestra scene with Soren! GAH MY FEELS!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. It probably leaves me sounding like a broken record but I cannot say it enough: TR's writing is on its league on its own, nothing comes close to it. It's so rare that I find myself soaking up every word and the brilliance and complexity of it all astounds me every single time.<br><br>The only thing that left me a little iffy is Nico's character and his intimacy with Nora but at this point of time, it's too early to say how he'll fit in nicely with the entire story arc. So I'm withholding judgement till the end of the series to see how it pans out because knowing TR, she just have tons of surprises up her sleeves. I cannot wait to read the rest of the series now!<br><br><i><u>The Saint</u> is the first in The White Year series and is recommended to read after finishing The Original Sinners series.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="7517114004210854462" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5439115409158346838"><b>5+ AMEN Stars</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Tiffany Reisz brought this series to a whole new level with this book, the writing was truly phenomenal! As much as a fan will want to go slow on this story it’s impossible and thus countless rereads will be taking place because this book was that good. Even if you have never read a single book in this series – I implore friends to give this book a shot because you will be hooked! I knew Nora and Søren’s back story was going to be good, but this blew my mind.<br/><br/>Nora is in </span>
  <span id="freeText5439115409158346838" style="display:none"><b>5+ AMEN Stars</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Tiffany Reisz brought this series to a whole new level with this book, the writing was truly phenomenal! As much as a fan will want to go slow on this story it’s impossible and thus countless rereads will be taking place because this book was that good. Even if you have never read a single book in this series – I implore friends to give this book a shot because you will be hooked! I knew Nora and Søren’s back story was going to be good, but this blew my mind.<br><br>Nora is in the Black Forest in a cabin dealing with a loss (a reader waits to the end of the story to find out who has departed). When someone seeking sanctuary knocks on her door it leads to a night of hot sex and our Mistress telling <s>a story</s> THE STORY of young Nora and Father Stearns.<br><br><b>
  <i>”You’re not a normal priest, are you?” He gave her a smile that hit her like a slap to the face and a kiss on the mouth all at once.<br><br>“My God, I hope not.”</i>
</b><br><br>Young Nora was <b>AMAZING</b>, she was feisty and smart and her interactions with Søren from the start were butterfly inducing … I dare any reader not to be swept away in their story.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I wish I could give you everything you wanted. But even a good gift is a bad gift if given at the wrong time.”</i>
</b><br><br>I don’t want to ruin the story by giving anything away, so I’m keeping this review very simple… <b>READ THIS BOOK</b> and fall in love with this unconventional story that has me questioning and making moral exceptions at every turn!<br><br><b>
  <i>”There is God, there is you and there is Kingsley. Those are my three nonnegotiables. You understand?”</i>
</b> <br><br>Thank you to Tiffany Reisz, Harlequin and NetGalley...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400324029ra/9663163.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*ARC kindly provided by Harlequin via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review*<br></i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9290413794428264082"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> "You're not a normal priest, are you?"<br/>"My God, I hope not." </i> </b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thesaintcollage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419323494i/13037988.png' alt=' photo thesaintcollage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I LOVE LOVE this author!!! I know going into any book she's written I will read something original and something that will suck me in right from the beginning. I love her writing style. <br/><br/><b> The Saint </b> is the sort of prequel to the Original Sinners series. Nora finds herself in Germany, grieving, and ends up telling the tale of how she and Søren met. I am so glad that Tiffany Reisz wrote this book, and although I know you</span>
  <span id="freeText9290413794428264082" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> "You're not a normal priest, are you?"<br>"My God, I hope not." </i> </b> <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/thesaintcollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419323494i/13037988.png" alt=" photo thesaintcollage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I LOVE LOVE this author!!! I know going into any book she's written I will read something original and something that will suck me in right from the beginning. I love her writing style. <br><br><b> The Saint </b> is the sort of prequel to the Original Sinners series. Nora finds herself in Germany, grieving, and ends up telling the tale of how she and Søren met. I am so glad that Tiffany Reisz wrote this book, and although I know you're techincally not supposed to, I wish I had read this book before reading <b> The Siren. </b><br><br>I know lots of you loved Søren right from the beginning, but it actually took until <b> The Prince </b> for me to like him, and that was the flashbacks from his school boy days. Plus, in <b> The Siren </b> the negative opinions of Wesley and Zack are so prominent, I feel like it influenced my original opinion of him. I loved Søren in this book (for the most part). I found him insightful, caring and at times, hilarious.<br><br><b> <i> “Well, a priest is better than a eunuch for advice, then. I’m guessing you still have all your original parts.”<br>“Warranty included.” </i> </b><br><br>In this book I really grew to love Søren and Nora's relationship. I had only liked Søren previously because of him and Kingsley (love them together). I still like Søren and Kingsley more than him and Nora.<br><br><b> <i> “When you hear music so beautiful it gives you chills, those are angel wings brushing against you.” </i> </b> <br><br>In this book I grew to hate Nora's mom. I honestly think that Nora was a victim of neglect because her mother didn't care about her, like at all.<br><br>Why not 5 stars? I had an issue with something Søren did. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ When he basically abandoned her for one year after she acted "childish". Whatever, the punishment did not fit the crime asshole. Good for you for teaching her you wouldn't be there for her when she needed you most. Ugh.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_740093251" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740093251" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740093251?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-love-my-friends">i-love-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=special-and-precious">special-and-precious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-taboo-forbidden-reads">dark-taboo-forbidden-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=drop-everything-and-read-it-now">drop-everything-and-read-it-now</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740093251" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6652168910548865099">Now live!! <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00H5I7ZNA/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B00H5I7ZNA&linkCode=as2&tag=bookvigirevi-20' rel='nofollow noopener'>AMAZON</a><br/><br/><b>5 stars!!</b><br/><br/><i>My ratings for this series have always been a bit skewed. I’ve rated the previous 4 books all 10 stars – highest rating I’ve ever given – and so for this book to only get 5 stars is the equivalent of a 4 out of 5 on a typical rating scale. I can’t find it in me to give any TOS book less than a 5 star rating because Tiffany’s writing is just that good.</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402589415i/9956928._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>As my #1 highly anticipated book of 2014, <u>The Saint</u> didn’t disappoint and it’s guaranteed to be one of my top reads of th</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6652168910548865099" style="display:none">Now live!! <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00H5I7ZNA/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B00H5I7ZNA&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=bookvigirevi-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br><b>5 stars!!</b><br><br><i>My ratings for this series have always been a bit skewed. I’ve rated the previous 4 books all 10 stars – highest rating I’ve ever given – and so for this book to only get 5 stars is the equivalent of a 4 out of 5 on a typical rating scale. I can’t find it in me to give any TOS book less than a 5 star rating because Tiffany’s writing is just that good.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402589415i/9956928._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>As my #1 highly anticipated book of 2014, <u>The Saint</u> didn’t disappoint and it’s guaranteed to be one of my top reads of the year. Reading this book made me nostalgic as the details of the Red Years Quartet came back to me. I’ve always been more than curious to know Søren and Nora’s backstory and wow, what a truly stunning and exquisite tale they have to tell.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Once there lived…a priest.”</i>
</b><br><br>The book is told mostly in Nora’s flashbacks as she reminisces about the very beginning with Kingsley’s son Nico so the entire book felt like a bedtime story – a yummy, humorous yet heartfelt bedtime story. <br><br>In the previous books, Nora (or Eleanor for when she was young) rarely talks about her past but we all know that she got in trouble a lot and was a rebel. Her family history is pretty bad – a criminal for a dad and a wannabe nun for a mom – and so growing up she knows what it’s like to feel rejected and neglected. She never expects to find anyone to care about her, much less do anything to protect her, not until she meets the new priest Søren, Father Stearns to everyone else. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re not a normal priest, are you?”<br>“My God, I hope not.”</i>
</b><br><br>I absolutely worshipped the first 50% of the book where I got to read Eleanor and Søren’s countless interactions and how she grew and matured under Søren’s guidance. Eleanor is such a spunky, feisty girl and Søren is a cool, calm, and collected man – they couldn’t be more different from one another and yet they complemented each other perfectly. I can’t count the number of times I laughed and re-read certain parts just so I could experience again the absolute joy of reading Tiffany’s words. <br><br>As much as I loved this book, it’s not my favorite and part of that reason is because nothing can top <u>The Angel</u> and <u>The Prince.</u> I thought the last 25% dragged a little and I guess the little romantic in me wanted more Eleanor and Søren time, not with everyone else involved. This book felt more like a snack than a full course meal like the Red Years books. However, one thing I just LOVED was that this book filled in the little gaps to the previous books: the meaning of the Rolls-Royce, where Nora’s nickname Little One came from, why Nora chose ‘Sutherlin’ as her writing name, etc…little things I wouldn’t have expected to have a story, Tiffany Reisz gave them one and it richened my reading experience. <br><br>I have to say, I have absolutely zero desire to be a part of the BDSM/erotica world Søren, Kingsley, and Eleanor are a part of, but damn, I just love being their observer. Perhaps it’s because I know I’ll never be in a world like theirs that makes their story and this series so compelling and enticing but whatever the reason, Tiffany Reisz’s books always leave me wanting more – more of her stories, more Søren, more Nora, just more. This author and series will remain my #1 favorite forever. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I give you forever, the least you can give me is everything.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>ARC provided by <u>Harlequin</u> via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6652168910548865099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer682157129002363570"> IT'S LIVE US: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1sZJn31'>http://amzn.to/1sZJn31</a><br/>Go check the blog tour and interview with Tiffany Reisz:<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/2014/06/blog-tour-saint-by-tiffany-reisz.html'>http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr...</a> <br/><br/><br/><b>6 NORA AND SOREN'S STARS<br/><br/>"Because there is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you,<br/>Eleanor.Nothing I wouldn't do to help you and nothing<br/>I wouldn't do to save you.Nothing."</b><br/><br/>This book was perfection!!I can't even express how much I loved it!I devoured it!It was emotional,intense and powerful!!This book will be a part of my heart and I will keep it till the end!OMG It was</span>
  <span id="freeText682157129002363570" style="display:none"> IT'S LIVE US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1sZJn31">http://amzn.to/1sZJn31</a><br>Go check the blog tour and interview with Tiffany Reisz:<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/2014/06/blog-tour-saint-by-tiffany-reisz.html">http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr...</a> <br><br><br><b>6 NORA AND SOREN'S STARS<br><br>"Because there is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you,<br>Eleanor.Nothing I wouldn't do to help you and nothing<br>I wouldn't do to save you.Nothing."</b><br><br>This book was perfection!!I can't even express how much I loved it!I devoured it!It was emotional,intense and powerful!!This book will be a part of my heart and I will keep it till the end!OMG It was amazing that we finally could learn more about how Nora met Soren and fell in love with him.And I fell in love with Soren too, once again!It's the biggest surprise for me because he is a little more kinky for my taste :)) but he managed to captivate me...and keep my interest!! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400107100i/9635891._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book split between now and then,with Nora and Nico (Kingsley's son), who honestly I wouldn't have problem if he didn't exist at all,because I was so focused on Nora and her stories that sometimes I forgot he was there with her!!Nora is telling stories about how see met Soren and Kingsley.Nora's and Søren's first collision and she tells us about the first few years after their meeting until Nora finally becomes Søren's...<br><br><b>"Once there lived....a Priest."</b><br><br>Nora as always was amazing!!She was such a badass!!!And I can understand why Soren was captivate with her from the begining!!Also I can understand why Nora was captivate with Soren!!<br>What can I say about Soren???OMG this sexy,kinky priest!!! *sigh* I love him!!They were born to be together!!Together they were pure magic!!Their relationship was pure and special!<br><br><b>“I want you.”<br> “You have me.” <br>“I want you inside me.”<br> “I’m always inside you, Little One.”<br><br><br>"Forever", She said. <br><br>And he said "Everything".</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403474288i/10097911._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You maybe won't believe me but while I was writing my review I was crying!!This series have touched me so much is so many ways!!Tiffany is so talented with her characters and the plot in her books!!She always make me hold my breath until the last page!!I'll definatelly will re-read The Original Sinners again and again!!! Kingsley was the typical Kingsley, just amazing :)) I can't wait to learn more and more about him!!I'm waiting for his book &lt;33<br><br><br>*ARC kindly provided by Harlequin via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review* </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/769733302" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/769733302?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780263245981" href="/book/show/21082347-the-saint">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=2014-favorite">2014-favorite</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769733302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16534861225728738614">It's live! <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00H5I7ZNA/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B00H5I7ZNA&linkCode=as2&tag=bookvigirevi-20' rel='nofollow noopener'>AMAZON</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402490309i/9944858._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I don't even know where to begin. This book. Is FUCKING awesome. I devoured it. It is perfection. Tiffany Reisz blew me away, again. The beginning of Eleanor and Søren was everything I had hoped for.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"It begins with a whimper but ends in a bang."</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>The Saint</i> will take you on a journey to the past and give you glimpses of the present. New characters are introduced and ashes are spread. As Eleanor tells the story of how she met Søren, and eventually Kingsley.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Once there lived </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16534861225728738614" style="display:none">It's live! <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00H5I7ZNA/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B00H5I7ZNA&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=bookvigirevi-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402490309i/9944858._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I don't even know where to begin. This book. Is FUCKING awesome. I devoured it. It is perfection. Tiffany Reisz blew me away, again. The beginning of Eleanor and Søren was everything I had hoped for.<br><br><b>
  <i>"It begins with a whimper but ends in a bang."</i>
</b><br><br><i>The Saint</i> will take you on a journey to the past and give you glimpses of the present. New characters are introduced and ashes are spread. As Eleanor tells the story of how she met Søren, and eventually Kingsley.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Once there lived a ... Priest."</i>
</b><br><br>From the moment Eleanor and Søren meet, they are drawn to each other. Only she is a teenager and he is a 29 year old priest. Young Eleanor is spunky, smart, curious, and a bit rebellious. She's just as entertaining as the Nora we have grown to love. And Søren, sigh, I just loved him. When Eleanor finds herself heading down the wrong path, Søren is there for her, determined to help her. They build a friendship, that grows into something so much more.<br><br><i>
  <b>"There is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you, Eleanor. Nothing I wouldn't do to help you and nothing I wouldn't do to save you. Nothing."</b>
</i><br><br>The sexual tension between these two was off the charts. I found myself constantly giddy with their interactions. I couldn't help but pull for them. These books keep me in constant moral conflict. I never know what to expect or even what I hope to happen.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402494493i/9945492._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="361" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If you are a fan of <i>The Original Sinners</i>, this is a must read. Seriously, READ IT. LOVE IT. You know you want too ;)<br> <br><i>
  <b>“Little One, to be with me is to hurt.” “To be without you would hurt more. It did hurt more. You won’t scare me off. I’m not afraid of you.”</b>
</i><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer633487067" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6811305097198745137">I feel sorry for the people who read the blurb for this thinking that it's the first in a series. For me, one of the highlights of my entire reading experience so far is seeing The 8th Circle through Zach's eyes and thinking this as Søren entered the room:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400160892ra/9642738.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>BUUUUUUUT, if you haven't read the blurb, just don't go there. Backtrack a bit, okay, a lot, and start with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532.The_Siren__The_Original_Sinners___1_' title='The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Siren</a> first, k?<br/><br/>Any Tiffany Reisz book I read is guaranteed fun times, this being no exception. Young Eleanor is just as entertaining</span>
  <span id="freeText6811305097198745137" style="display:none">I feel sorry for the people who read the blurb for this thinking that it's the first in a series. For me, one of the highlights of my entire reading experience so far is seeing The 8th Circle through Zach's eyes and thinking this as Søren entered the room:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400160892ra/9642738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BUUUUUUUT, if you haven't read the blurb, just don't go there. Backtrack a bit, okay, a lot, and start with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532.The_Siren__The_Original_Sinners___1_" title="The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a> first, k?<br><br>Any Tiffany Reisz book I read is guaranteed fun times, this being no exception. Young Eleanor is just as entertaining to read about as the grown-up Nora, if not more interesting. She already has the humor, the sensuality, and even the rebellion and stupidity that get her into trouble. But she also has remnants of innocence and a smidge of destructive behavior that make her more intense at this age. She's curious and experimental - definitely a dangerous combination. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Don't worry. No boys for me."<br>"Girls?" He gave her a steady, "is there something you need to tell me" stare.<br>She shook her head.<br>"No girls, either."<br>"Thank, God."<br>"I want a man."<br>"Where's my shotgun?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This might be as close as it gets to a TOS book being labelled as a romance. <b>I cannot stop squeeing the entire time Eleanor and Søren get into those sexual-tension-charged conversations!</b> I know it's wrong to feel this about a fifteen year old but damn, this was so hot! If it was someone else, I'd be disgusted, but these are people I know and love so reading about their past only excited me. I didn't have the gnawing fear or worry that I felt when I read the other books in this series. Maybe it's because the story only showed a glimpse of how dangerous Søren is. Or maybe it's because I now know what he's capable of and the lengths he would go to for the people he loves. But I was still very much in awe of him here. He truly is the most magnetic male character I've ever come across. I turn into a puddle on the floor just reading about his piercing stares and gazes.<br><br>I think my favourite feature of a prequel is the multiple references to events that you already know about. It's like sharing an inside joke with a close friend. Or in this case, smiling deviously because I know something that Eleanor doesn't know yet. I thought the scene where she thought up of synonyms for the word <i>thrust</i> was hilarious!<br><br>I really have to credit Tiffany Reisz for turning this into something totally unexpected. Before I read this I thought it would be a "once upon a time" story since we all knew that it was about The White Years. But no, there has to be some mindfuckery involved. I nearly fell off my chair when I started reading and discovered that the story is in <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[THE PRESENT TIME!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Good gawd. And this introduction of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Nico <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> smells like trouble to me. But what are chances that he's also sexy and into kink? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And also into Nora? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I don't know how I feel about him yet. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I don't know if I'd be okay if Nora fell for him because of Wesley and the bond of the unholy Trinity that I don't want to break if King disapproves. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>For some reason, it never occurred to me that the box contained <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Søren's ashes. I entertained the thought of it containing Nora's collar, that they may have broken up. But no, I didn't think Søren died. I just can't imagine a Sinners world where he does not exist. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>I guess my only issue with this book was the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[storytelling part. I thought it was great, but not original since we already got that in The Prince and The Mistress. I didn't get chills when Søren told Kingsley how he found <i>her</i> because that was so brilliantly told in The Prince already. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Tiffany's biggest competition is herself, and I don't think this one outdid The Prince. I shouldn't compare, I know, but that book was so powerful and forever etched in my memory that I can't help it. <br><br>Still an amazing read, nevertheless. And just as with any other Tiffany Reisz book, this left me wanting more. I can't wait for The King!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/592914.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Advanced copy provided by Harlequin Mira through Net Galley. Thank you for the opportunity to read and review!</i><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><br><b>All these <i>The Mistress</i> status updates are making me excited for this!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424217ra/845659.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You call her Little One?"<br><br>"I always have. She was a teenager when we met. A very ill-mannered teenager. She demanded to know why I was so tall. She insinuated I had grown this tall simply for attention."<br><br>"Only Nora could be rude and flirtatious at the same time."<br><br>"I explained to her that I was tall so I could hear God's voice better. And since I was taller and could hear Him better, she should always listen to me. That didn't sit very well with her. She retorted the next day with a verse from Psalm 114. <b>'The Lord keeps the little ones.'</b> Her biblical proof that God prefers short people. I started calling her Little One after that..."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Eleanor, you're supposed to be in school." He didn't even look up at her from his work as he squatted on the ground and covered the roots of the sapling in black earth.<br><br>"It was a life-or-death situation. If I stayed in school, I would have killed myself."<br><br>"As suicide is a mortal sin, I'll absolve you for cutting class. But you know you are also not supposed to be at the rectory." He didn't sound at all angry or disappointed, only amused by her as usual.<br><br>"I'm outside the fence. I'm not at the rectory - I'm just near it. What are you doing anyway?"<br><br>"Planting trees."<br><br>"Obviously, but why? Are the two million trees around us not enough for you?"<br><br>"Not quite. You can still see the rectory from the church."<br><br>"Is that a bad thing?"<br><br>Søren stood up and walked over to the fence. Nora remembered how her heart had hammered at that moment. She thought for certain he could hear it beating through her chest.<br><br>Face-to-face with only the fence and a fourteen-year age difference between them, Søren pulled of his sunglasses and met her eyes.<br><br>"I like my privacy." He gave her a conspiratorial smile.<br><br>"It'll take years before you get any." Søren arched an eyebrow at her, and she'd blushed. "Privacy, I mean. Trees take forever to grow."<br><br>"Not these. Empress trees and this particular species of willow are some of the fastest growing."<br><br><u>"In a hurry for your privacy?"<br><br>"I can wait."<br><br>Something in his eyes and his voice told her that they weren't talking about the trees anymore. I can wait, he'd said and looked at her with a gaze so intimate she felt as if it was his hand on her face and not just his eyes.<br><br>She summoned her courage and returned the gaze.<br><br>"So can I."</u></i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415774ra/820883.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797335i/630329._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/906020947?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=arc">arc</a>,
